### 主要投诉
- 呕吐

### 现病史
- ___ 患有胃出口梗阻和幽门肿块，最近在门诊就诊，现在出现恶心/呕吐。该患者最近因相同症状入院，上周在诊所就诊。她出院时已恢复正常并确保安全。 EUS 活检显示高度不典型增生和明显的食管炎。她已被预约进行诊断性腹腔镜检查以及可能的远端胃切除术与胃空肠旁路术，但昨天发生了几次非血性非胆汁性呕吐，今天早上发生了一次，促使她去急诊室就诊。目前，她感觉良好，没有疼痛，但感到恶心，感觉胃里好像有东西被卡住。患者直到昨天才定期排便，并且仍在放屁。否认发烧、寒战。 

### 系统审查（准入前）
- 出现恶心和呕吐。
- 否认发烧或发冷。
- 否认腹痛。
- 报告有规律的排便和排气。

### 既往病史

- Radiology Note: FINDINGS:
  LOWER CHEST: Please refer to separate CT chest dictated on the same day for
  findings regarding the thorax.
  
  ABDOMEN:
  
  HEPATOBILIARY: The liver demonstrates homogenous attenuation throughout. 
  There is no evidence of focal lesions.  There is no evidence of intrahepatic
  or extrahepatic biliary dilatation.  The gallbladder is within normal limits.
  
  PANCREAS: The pancreas has normal attenuation throughout, without evidence of
  focal lesions or pancreatic ductal dilatation.  There is no peripancreatic
  stranding.
  
  SPLEEN:  A 1 cm accessory spleen is noted.  The spleen shows normal size and
  attenuation throughout, without evidence of focal lesions.
  
  ADRENALS: The right and left adrenal glands are normal in size and shape.
  
  URINARY: The kidneys are of normal and symmetric size with normal nephrogram. 
  A 1.5 x 1.2 cm (02:58) incompletely characterized left lower pole renal cystic
  lesion is stable and measures 48 Hounsfield units.  Additional bilateral
  subcentimeter renal hypodensities are too small to characterize.  No
  hydronephrosis.  There is no perinephric abnormality.
  
  GASTROINTESTINAL: Multiple fluid-filled dilated small bowel loops measuring up
  to 5.3 cm in a patient who is status post partial gastrectomy with
  gastrojejunostomy and transition point at the gastrojejunostomy, worrisome for
  afferent limb closed loop obstruction.  The stomach and distal esophagus are
  also distended with contrast (series 2, image 43, 34).  Small amount of free
  fluid. Preserved mucosal hyper enhancement. No pneumatosis. Gastrojejunostomy
  tube is in appropriate position with a collapsed efferent (enteric) limb.  The
  colon is unremarkable and decompressed. The appendix is not visualized,
  however no secondary signs of acute appendicitis.
  
  PELVIS: Air within the urinary bladder is expected in a patient who is status
  post Foley placement.  The distal ureters are unremarkable.  There is small
  amount of nonhemorrhagic free fluid in the pelvis.
  
  REPRODUCTIVE ORGANS: Uterus is not visualized.  No large adnexal masses seen.
  
  LYMPH NODES: There is no retroperitoneal or mesenteric lymphadenopathy.  There
  is no pelvic or inguinal lymphadenopathy.
  
  VASCULAR: There is no abdominal aortic aneurysm.  Mild atherosclerotic disease
  is noted.
  
  BONES:  Moderate multilevel degenerative changes are seen throughout the
  thoracolumbar spine including large anterior flowing osteophytes, and
  subchondral sclerosis.  There is no evidence of worrisome osseous lesions or
  acute fracture.
  
  SOFT TISSUES: Anasarca is noted.  Midline staples are present.  The abdominal
  and pelvic wall is otherwise within normal limits.
  
  IMPRESSION:
  1.  Findings worrisome for afferent limb closed loop obstruction in a patient
  who is status post partial gastrectomy with gastrojejunostomy.  Transition
  point at gastrojejunostomy.  Small amount of free fluid. Preserved mucosal
  hyperenhancement. No pneumatosis.
  2.  Distended stomach and esophagus with oral contrast may reflect gastric
  outlet obstruction, also at the gastrojejunostomy.
  3.  Percutaneous gastrojejunostomy tube in appropriate position, extending
  into the collapsed efferent (enteric) limb.
  4.  Stable intermediate density 1.5 cm left renal lesion, incompletely
  characterized.
  
  NOTIFICATION:  The findings were discussed by Dr. ___ with Dr. ___
  on the telephone on ___ at 3:20 ___, 5 minutes after discovery of the
  findings.
- Radiology Note: FINDINGS:
  Again seen are 1 x 0.7 cm and 0.5 x 0.5 cm right and left thyroid lobe nodules
  respectively, which are unchanged since prior examination(2:4).  No
  supraclavicular, axillary, mediastinal and hilar lymph nodes are not enlarged.
  Aorta and pulmonary arteries are normal size. Cardiac configuration is normal
  and there is mild coronary artery calcification.
  
  There is interval increase in small bilateral non hemorrhagic pleural
  effusions with associated compressive atelectasis.  Left pleural effusion is
  intermediate density measuring 31 Hounsfield units suggestive of an exudative
  component.  The lungs are notable for bilateral lower lobe opacities.
  
  The soft tissues are unremarkable.  Patient is status post gastrectomy, and
  the esophagus is mildly dilated and fluid-filled.  A 0.7 x 0.6 cm (4:160)
  well-circumscribed hyperdensity adjacent to the GE junction with preserved fat
  plane between the esophagus is consistent with a small lymph node.
  
  Visualized osseous structures are notable for degenerative changes throughout
  the thoracic spine with disc space narrowing, subchondral sclerosis, and
  anterior osteophyte formation.  A chronic left acromion fracture is noted.  No
  acute fracture.
  
  Please refer to separate CT chest for dedicated findings within the
  abdomen/pelvis.
  
  IMPRESSION:
  1.  Status post gastrectomy with associated postsurgical changes and mildly
  dilated fluid-filled esophagus.  Of note patient is at increased risk for
  aspiration.
  2.  New small bilateral pleural effusions with possible exudative left pleural
  effusion.
  3.  Bilateral lower lobe opacities are most consistent with atelectasis,
  clinical correlation recommended to assess for superimposed infection.
  4.  Persistent bilateral thyroid lobe nodules largest measuring 1 cm within
  the right thyroid lobe.  If clinically indicated and not previously assessed,

  LOWER CHEST: An enteric tube courses through the distal esophagus and
  terminates in the anterior gastric lumen.  There are stable left greater than
  right small layering pleural effusions with adjacent relaxation basilar
  atelectasis.  There is no pericardial effusion.
  
  CT ABDOMEN:
  
  HEPATOBILIARY: Again seen is a heterogeneous enhancement pattern of the liver,
  with an ill-defined area of irregular enhancement affecting the left hepatic
  lobe (for example see series 2, image 26).  Additional irregular hypodensities
  in segments IV A/B (series 2, image 27) are also similar in appearance, and
  abut the gallbladder fossa.  Previously demonstrated right hepatic
  hypodensities are less well-defined; for example, see series 2, image 12 for
  lesion near the liver dome which is decreased in conspicuity since prior.  An
  additional similar hypodensity is seen in segment VIII (series 2, image 25),
  less conspicuous.  There is a persistent, heterogeneous 2.5 x 2.4 cm
  phlegmonous appearing collection in the gallbladder fossa (series 2, image
  29), unchanged since prior.  The gallbladder is surgically absent.  Mild
  central and left predominant intrahepatic biliary ductal dilation is
  persistent.  The portal vein is patent.
  
  PANCREAS: There is stable prominence of the proximal main pancreatic duct
  measuring 4 mm.  Otherwise, the pancreas enhances homogeneously. There is no
  peripancreatic stranding.
  
  SPLEEN: There is no splenomegaly or focal splenic lesion.
  
  ADRENALS: The adrenal glands are normal.
  
  URINARY: Again seen is a stable 1.7 x 0.9 cm intermediate density left lower
  pole lesion (series 2, image 39).  An additional 2.1 x 1.7 cm (series 2, image
  33) peripherally calcified right complex cyst is again noted.  There are left
  parapelvic cysts.  Smaller bilateral renal cortical hypodensities are too
  small characterize accurately by CT.  Otherwise, the kidneys enhance normally
  and symmetrically.  There is no hydronephrosis.
  
  GASTROINTESTINAL:  Two (2) JP drains are seen in unchanged location entering
  via the right hemiabdomen terminating around the proximal afferent limb.  The
  patient is status post distal gastrectomy with Roux-en-Y reconstruction.  A
  percutaneous gastrojejunostomy tube is seen in unchanged, appropriate location
  with the balloon inflated in the distal remaining stomach.  The distal tip
  terminates near the JJ anastomosis.  Again seen is hypoenhancement of the
  proximal a pharynx limb (series 2, image 43), with adjacent surgical suture,
  concerning for ischemic bowel.  An additional segment of small bowel are no
  the anterior midline is hypoenhancing, also again concerning for ischemia
  (series 2, image 57).  The JJ anastomosis itself appears intact and
  unremarkable.  The remaining small bowel loops are distended and filled with
  fluid but not frankly dilated.  The colon is decompressed.  Again noted is
  what appears to be marked hypoenhancement of the distal ascending and
  transverse colon (for example see series 2 image 47 and image 40), concerning
  for ischemia.  A transition to normal enhancement of the distal transverse
  colon is noted (series 2, image 44).  This is concerning for ischemia.  The
  distal colon is decompressed, but unremarkable.
  
  Uniform enhancement of the peritoneal lining is concerning for peritonitis,
  most apparent in the dependent portion of the peritoneal cavity.
  
  VASCULAR AND LYMPH NODES: Mild atherosclerotic disease is most prominent in
  the infrarenal abdominal aorta.  The abdominal aorta is normal in caliber
  without evidence of aneurysm or dilation.  Major proximal tributaries,
  including the imaged course of the SMA, are patent.
  
  Again seen is diffuse ascites, small volume.  There is no free intraperitoneal
  air.
  
  CT PELVIS:
  A Foley catheter is inflated in the bladder lumen, which otherwise
  decompressed.  Otherwise, the imaged pelvic organs are unremarkable.  There is
  no pelvic sidewall, iliac chain, or inguinal lymphadenopathy.
  
  MUSCULOSKELETAL: Diffuse anasarca is again noted.  There is severe
  thoracolumbar spine degenerative change.  Alignment is normal.  No concerning
  focal lytic or sclerotic osseous lesions are seen
  
  IMPRESSION:
  1. Persistent hypoenhancement of multiple loops of small and large bowel,
  including the proximal afferent limb as well as the distal ascending and
  proximal transverse colon, as above.  Findings concerning for small bowel and
  colonic ischemia.
  2. Uniform enhancement of the peritoneum most apparent in the pelvis is
  concerning for peritonitis.
  3. Stable JP drain location surrounding the proximal efferent limb.  Stable
  location of enteric and gastrojejunostomy tubes.
  4. Stable heterogeneity of the liver, primarily affecting the left hepatic
  lobe.  While some of these areas, particularly near segments II and ___
  reflect retraction injury in the setting of recent surgery, more medial
  hypodensities abutting the region of the gallbladder fossa collection may
  represent developing abscess.
  5. Persistent small volume ascites.  Diffuse anasarca.
  6. Unchanged 2.5 x 2.4 cm heterogeneous, phlegmonous appearing collection in
  gallbladder fossa.
  7. Unchanged mild central and left intrahepatic biliary ductal dilation.
  8. Stable small to moderate left and small right layering pleural effusions
  with adjacent bilateral lower lobe relaxation atelectasis.

问题与答案

时间点 2143-05-31 08:00，基于该患者的临床证据，应开具以下哪些药物？

A.Dextrose 5% in Water (D5W); 1000 mL; route=IV错误
5% 葡萄糖水溶液 (D5W) - 错误：D5W 是低渗的，会加重第三间隙大和胸腔积液患者的自由水超负荷和低钠血症风险。
B.Norepinephrine; 8 mg; route=IV DRIP错误
去甲肾上腺素 - 错误：去甲肾上腺素会过度升高心脏后负荷，并且在没有分布性休克的情况下，体弱的术后患者有发生快速心律失常的风险。
C.Dextrose 5% in Lactated Ringer’s (D5LR); 1000 mL; route=IV错误
乳酸林格氏液 (D5LR) 中的 5% 葡萄糖 - 错误：D5LR 会给有高血糖和乳酸性酸中毒风险的患者增加不必要的葡萄糖和乳酸负荷，从而恶化代谢控制，而无法有效恢复血管内钠。
D.Hydrochlorothiazide; 25 mg; route=PO错误
氢氯噻嗪 - 错误：噻嗪类利尿剂会进一步减少血管内容量，并使该低灌注手术患者的肾前性氮质血症恶化。
E.0.9% Sodium Chloride; 250 mL; route=IV DRIP正确
0.9% 氯化钠 - 正确：0.9% 氯化钠静脉滴注作为维持液。实验室检查结果显示钠正常，BUN 升高，提示肾前性生理，持续服用利尿剂并伴有胸腔积液，表明可能存在血管内容量减少。等渗盐水的目的是维持血流动力学稳定性和肾灌注，而不是复苏急性低血压。
F.Dobutamine; 250 mg; route=IV DRIP错误
多巴酚丁胺 - 错误：多巴酚丁胺主要增加正性肌力和心率，而不是全身血管阻力，这会加重血管舒张性休克生理学中的低血压。
G.PHENYLEPHrine; 60 mg; route=IV DRIP正确
去氧肾上腺素 - 正确：静脉输注去氧肾上腺素以支持血流动力学。患者的升压药需求史和 BUN 升高意味着持续的灌注不足。去氧肾上腺素用于在循环不稳定期间维持血压和终末器官灌注。

请返回问卷页面对以上答案和解释进行评估。
